My doctor was worried and talked of possible liver damage.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;He suspected one of the suplements that I am taking saying that suplements are not regulated by the FDA and that many are made outside of the U.S., mostly in China, where other ingredients are added for one reason or the other.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;To shorten the story a bit, upon a retest my liver ensymes returned to 25 / 27.  I had removed the suplements that I was taking.
